\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ file\ implements\ a\ bitset\ much\ like\ the\ C++\ std::bitset\ class.\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ primary\ distinctions\ between\ this\ list\ and\ std::bitset\ are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ bitset\ is\ more\ efficient\ than\ some\ other\ std::bitset\ implementations,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ notably\ the\ bitset\ that\ comes\ with\ Microsoft\ and\ other\ 1st\ party\ platforms.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ bitset\ is\ savvy\ to\ an\ environment\ that\ doesn't\ have\ exception\ handling,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ as\ is\ sometimes\ the\ case\ with\ console\ or\ embedded\ environments.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ bitset\ is\ savvy\ to\ environments\ in\ which\ 'unsigned\ long'\ is\ not\ the\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ most\ efficient\ integral\ data\ type.\ std::bitset\ implementations\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ unsigned\ long,\ even\ if\ it\ is\ an\ inefficient\ integer\ type.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ bitset\ removes\ as\ much\ function\ calls\ as\ practical,\ in\ order\ to\ allow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ debug\ builds\ to\ run\ closer\ in\ speed\ and\ code\ footprint\ to\ release\ builds.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ bitset\ doesn't\ support\ string\ functionality.\ We\ can\ add\ this\ if\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ it\ is\ deemed\ useful.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
